NOTICE

MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
Form No. 155
[Members Voluntary Winding-up]
ITI CAPITAL MARKETS LTD.
(Registered office: Century Centre, 75, TTK Road, Alwarpet, Chennai-600 018)
Notice convening final meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of Companies Act 1956 that a general meeting of the members
of the above-named company will be held at Century Centre, 75 TTK Road, Alwarpet, Chennai-600 018 on the 30th day
of November 2016 at 12 o’clock in the noon for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing the manner
in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any explanation
that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company the manner in which the
books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
26th October 2016.

ITI Capital Markets Ltd,.

JAYARAM, S.
Liquidator.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
